3 import scala.concurrent._
4 import javax.inject._
5 import play.api._

7 import play.api.libs.json._
8 import play.api.mvc._

25 /**
26  * This Controller handles API Requests concerning events
27  */
28 class EventController @Inject()(cc: ControllerComponents,
29                                 protected val dbConfigProvider: DatabaseConfigProvider,
30                                 val silhouette: Silhouette[AuthEnv],
31                                 val organizerService: OrganizerService,
32                                 val userService: UserService,
33                                 eventService: EventService,
34                                 locationService: LocationService,
35                                 importService: ImportService)
36     (implicit context: ExecutionContext)
37     extends AbstractController(cc)
38     with HasDatabaseConfigProvider[JdbcProfile]
39     with Util {
40 
41   val log = Logger("api.event")
42 
43   def getEvent(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
44     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
45 
46     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
47 
48     db.run(q.detailed).map(x => x.headOption match {
49       case Some(r) => Ok(Json.toJson(r))
50       case _ => NotFound
51     })
52   }
53 
54   def searchEvents(search: Option[String], location: Option[Int], category: Option[Int],
55                    sort: Option[String], sortDir: Boolean, from: Option[Timestamp], to: Option[Timestamp]) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
56     log.debug("Rest request to search events")
57     
58     val q = for {
59       e <- event if similar(e.name,search.getOrElse("").bind) || search.getOrElse("").bind === ""
60                  if e.categories.filter(_.id === category.getOrElse(-1)).exists || category.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
61                  if e.locationId - location.getOrElse(-1).bind === 0 || location.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
62                  if e.from >= from.getOrElse(new Timestamp(0,0,0,0,0,0,0)) && e.from <= to.getOrElse(new Timestamp(4000,0,0,0,0,0,0))
63                  if e.to.getOrElse(plus(e.from,oneDay)) >= currentTimestamp
64     } yield e
65 
66 
67 
68     val s = q.sortColumn(sort,sortDir).queryPaged.detailed
69     returnPaged(s,q,db)
70   }
71 
72   def getNearby(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
73     log.debug("Rest request to get events nearby another event")
74 
75     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
76 
77     db.run(q.detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
78       case Some(e) => {
79         val q = EventTable.event.join(LocationTable.location).on(_.locationId === _.id)
80           .sortBy(y => geoDistance(e.location.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, e.location.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, 
81               y._2.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f), y._2.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f)))
82           .map(_._1).filter(y => y.id =!= e.id && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
83         val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
84         returnPaged(s,q,db)
85       }
86       case None => Future(NotFound)
87     }
88   }
89 
90   def getSameViewed(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
91     log.debug("Rest request to get events other participants also visit")
92 
93     val q = ParticipantCountView.participantCount.filter(_.id === id.bind)
94       .join(EventTable.event).on(_.event_fk === _.id)
95       .sortBy(y => y._1.count.desc).map(_._2)
96       .filter(y => y.id =!= id.bind && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
97 
98     val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
99 
100     returnPaged(s,q,db)
101   }
102 
103   def deleteEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { (request,organizer) =>
104     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
105 
106     val q = event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).delete
107 
108     db.run(q).map {
109       case 0 => NotFound
110       case x => Ok(Json.toJson(x))
111     }
112   }
113 
114   def createEvent() = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
115     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
116       form => {
117         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
118       },
119       data => {
120         log.debug("Rest request to create event")
121 
122         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
123 
124         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
125 
126         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(
127           data.categories.map {
128             case cat =>
129               cat.id match {
130                 case None => insertAndReturn[Category,CategoryTable](CategoryTable.category,cat).map(x => List(x).seq)
131                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
132               }
133           }).map(_.flatten)
134 
135         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
136           case ((images,categories),Some(location)) => {
137             val event = Event(None, data.name, data.from, data.to,
138                               data.description, data.shortDescription,
139                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1),
140                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax)
141             db.run(insertAndReturn[Event,EventTable](EventTable.event,event)).map(r => (r,images,categories))
142           }.flatMap { case (event,images,categories) =>
143               val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event,img._2))
144               val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
145               val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
146               db.run(imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed)
147           }.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x.head)))
148           case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
149         }
150       })
151   }
152 
153   def updateEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
154     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
155       form => {
156         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
157       },
158       data => {
159         log.debug("Rest request to update event")
160 
161         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
162 
163         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
164 
165         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(
166           data.categories.map {
167             case cat =>
168               cat.id match {
169                 case None => insertAndReturn[Category,CategoryTable](CategoryTable.category,cat).map(x => List(x).seq)
170                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
171               }
172           }).map(_.flatten)
173 
174         val eventQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).result.map(_.headOption)
175 
176         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery).zip(eventQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
177           case (((images,categories),Some(event)),Some(location)) => {
178             val event = Event(Some(id), data.name, data.from, data.to,
179                               data.description, data.shortDescription,
180                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1),
181                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax)
182 
183             val getQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id)
184 
185             db.run(getQuery.update(event) >> getQuery.result.map(_.head))
186               .map(r => Some((r,images,categories)))
187           }
188           case _ => Future.successful(None)
189         }.flatMap {
190           case Some((event,images,categories)) => {
191             val dropImages = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity.filter(x => x.entityId === id && x.entityType === EntityType.Event).delete
192             val dropCategories = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory.filter(x => x.eventID === id).delete
193             val dropQuery = dropImages.zip(dropCategories)
194 
195             val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event, img._2))
196             val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
197             val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
198             db.run(dropQuery >> imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed).map(x => Some(x))
199           }
200           case None => Future.successful(None)
201         }.map {
202           case Some(e) => Ok(Json.toJson(e))
203           case None => BadRequest
204         }
205       })
206   }
207 
208   def insertCSV = organizerRequest(parse.multipartFormData) { case (request,organizer) =>
209     log.debug("Rest request to insert events by csv")
210 
211     request.body.file("csv").map { case x =>
212       val file = x.ref.path.toFile()
213 
214       eventService.insertCSV(file,organizer)
215      }.map(_.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))).headOption.getOrElse(Future.successful(BadRequest))
216   }
217 
218   def participate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
219     log.debug("Rest request to participate in event")
220 
221     val q = (event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind).result)
222       .zip(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).result)
223 
224     db.run(q).map(x => (x._1.headOption,x._2.headOption)).flatMap {
225       case (Some(e),None) => {
226         db.run(ParticipantTable.participant += ((user.id.getOrElse(-1),id)))
227         Future.successful(Ok)
228       }
229       case (Some(e),Some(p)) => Future.successful(Conflict)
230       case (None,_) => Future.successful(BadRequest)
231     }
232   }
233 
234   def unparticipate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
235     log.debug("Rest request to unparticipate in event")
236 
237     db.run(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).delete)
238       .flatMap {
239       case 1 => {
240         Future.successful(Ok)
241       }
242       case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
243     }
244   }
245 
246   def getSliderEvents = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
247     log.debug("Rest request to get events for slider")
248 
249     db.run(SliderEventTable.sliderEvent.sortBy(_.number).flatMap(_.event).detailed).map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))
250   }
251 
252   def importFacebookEvent(url: String) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { case (request,organizer) =>
253     log.debug("Rest request to import event from url")
254 
255     importService.getEvent(url, request.identity)
256       .map(x => x.map(y => Ok(Json.toJson(y))).getOrElse(BadRequest))
257   }
